CStrings:
+ "\n\n    async function filteredTextSnippet(element) {\n        const skipTags = new Set(['script', 'style', 'noscript', 'head', 'meta', 'link', 'title']);\n        if (skipTags.has(element.tagName.toLowerCase()))\n            return '';\n\n        let text = '';\n        for (const node of element.childNodes) {\n            if (node.nodeType === Node.TEXT_NODE)\n                text += node.nodeValue;\n        }\n\n        text = text.replace(/\\s+/g, ' ').trim();\n        if (!text)\n            return '';\n\n        const filtered = await filterText(text);\n        if (!filtered)\n            return '';\n\n        const half = Math.floor(maxSnippetLength / 2);\n        const snippet = filtered.length <= maxSnippetLength ? filtered : filtered.slice(0, half) + '…' + filtered.slice(-(half - 1));\n        return ' \"' + snippet + '\"';\n    }\n\n    const filterTerms = searchTerms.map((term) => term.toLowerCase());\n\n    function elementMatchesTerms(element) {\n        const skipTags = new Set(['script', 'style', 'noscript', 'head', 'meta', 'link', 'title']);\n        if (skipTags.has(element.tagName.toLowerCase()))\n            return false;\n\n        const tag = element.tagName.toLowerCase();\n        if (filterTerms.some((term) => tag.includes(term)))\n            return true;\n\n        for (const cls of element.classList) {\n            if (filterTerms.some((term) => cls.toLowerCase().includes(term)))\n                return true;\n        }\n\n        const id = element.getAttribute('id');\n        if (id && filterTerms.some((term) => id.toLowerCase().includes(term)))\n            return true;\n\n        const role = element.getAttribute('role');\n        if (role && filterTerms.some((term) => role.toLowerCase().includes(term)))\n            return true;\n\n        for (const attribute of element.attributes) {\n            if (attribute.name.startsWith('data-')) {\n                if (filterTerms.some((term) => attribute.name.toLowerCase().includes(term)))\n                    return true;\n                if (attribute.value && filterTerms.some((term) => attribute.value.toLowerCase().includes(term)))\n                    return true;\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (element.children.length === 0) {\n            const text = element.textContent.replace(/\\s+/g, ' ').trim().toLowerCase();\n            if (text && filterTerms.some((term) => text.includes(term)))\n                return true;\n        }\n\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    function buildAncestorChain(element) {\n        if (element.getAttribute('id'))\n            return [element];\n\n        const chain = [element];\n        let ancestor = element.parentElement;\n        let steps = 0;\n\n        while (ancestor && ancestor !== document.documentElement && steps < maxAncestorSteps) {\n            chain.unshift(ancestor);\n            steps++;\n            if (ancestor.getAttribute('id'))\n                break;\n            ancestor = ancestor.parentElement;\n        }\n\n        return chain;\n    }\n\n    const root = rootSelector ? document.querySelector(rootSelector) : document.body;\n    if (!root)\n        return { header: rootSelector ? 'Error: rootSelector did not match any element.' : 'Error: No document body.', content: '' };\n\n    if (rootSelector && document.querySelectorAll(rootSelector).length > 1)\n        return { header: 'Error: rootSelector matched multiple elements — use a more specific selector.', content: '' };\n\n    const matchingElements = [];\n    const walker = document.createTreeWalker(root, NodeFilter.SHOW_ELEMENT);\n\n    let node = walker.nextNode();\n    while (node && matchingElements.length < maxResults) {\n        if (elementMatchesTerms(node))\n            matchingElements.push(node);\n        node = walker.nextNode();\n    }\n\n    let totalCount = matchingElements.length;\n    while (node) {\n        if (elementMatchesTerms(node))\n            totalCount++;\n        node = walker.nextNode();\n    }\n\n    if (matchingElements.length === 0)\n        return { header: 'No elements found matching search terms.', content: '' };\n\n    const allChains = [];\n\n    for (const element of matchingElements) {\n        const chain = buildAncestorChain(element);\n        const matchIndex = chain.length - 1;\n\n        const lines = [];\n        for (let i = 0; i < chain.length; i++) {\n            const isMatch = i === matchIndex;\n            const elementSelector = await filteredSelectorForElement(chain[i], includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers);\n            if (!elementSelector)\n                continue;\n            lines.push('\\t'.repeat(i) + elementSelector + (isMatch ? await filteredTextSnippet(chain[i]) : ''));\n        }\n\n        const children = Array.from(element.children);\n        for (const child of children.slice(0, 10)) {\n            const childSelector = await filteredSelectorForElement(child, includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers);\n            if (childSelector)\n                lines.push('\\t'.repeat(matchIndex + 1) + childSelector + await filteredTextSnippet(child));\n        }\n\n        if (children.length > 10)\n            lines.push('\\t'.repeat(matchIndex + 1) + '…');\n\n        allChains.push({ lines: lines, matchIndex: matchIndex });\n    }\n\n    const chainCounts = new Map();\n    const uniqueChains = [];\n    for (const chain of allChains) {\n        const rendered = chain.lines.join('\\n');\n        if (chainCounts.has(rendered)) {\n            chainCounts.set(rendered, chainCounts.get(rendered) + 1);\n        } else {\n            chainCounts.set(rendered, 1);\n            uniqueChains.push(chain);\n        }\n    }\n\n    const renderedChains = uniqueChains.slice(0, maxResults).map(chain => {\n        const rendered = chain.lines.join('\\n');\n        const count = chainCounts.get(rendered);\n        if (count === 1)\n            return rendered;\n\n        const lines = [...chain.lines];\n        lines[chain.matchIndex] += ' ×' + count;\n\n        return lines.join('\\n');\n    });\n\n    const header = totalCount === 1 ? '1 matching element:'\n        : totalCount + ' matching elements' + (totalCount > maxResults ? ' (showing first ' + maxResults + '):' : ':');\n    return { header: header, content: renderedChains.join('\\n---\\n') };\n})();"
+ "\n\n    const cssX = x * window.innerWidth;\n    const cssY = y * window.innerHeight;\n\n    const elements = document.elementsFromPoint(cssX, cssY);\n    const relevant = elements.filter((element) => element !== document.documentElement).slice(0, maxElements);\n\n    if (relevant.length === 0)\n        return { header: `No elements at (${x}, ${y}). The point may be outside the viewport.`, content: '' };\n\n    const ordered = [...relevant].reverse();\n\n    const lines = [];\n    for (const [i, element] of ordered.entries()) {\n        const selector = await filteredSelectorForElement(element, includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers);\n        if (selector)\n            lines.push('\\t'.repeat(i) + selector);\n    }\n\n    if (lines.length === 0)\n        return { header: `No selectors available for elements at (${x}, ${y}).`, content: '' };\n\n    let textNode = null;\n    try {\n        const caretPosition = document.caretPositionFromPoint(cssX, cssY);\n        if (caretPosition && caretPosition.offsetNode && caretPosition.offsetNode.nodeType === Node.TEXT_NODE)\n            textNode = caretPosition.offsetNode;\n    } catch (error) { }\n\n    if (textNode) {\n        const rawText = (textNode.nodeValue ?? '' : 's'} at (${x}, ${y}):`;\n    return { header: header, content: lines.join('\\n') };\n})();"
+ "\n\n    const lines = [];\n\n    async function walk(element, depth, precomputedSelector) {\n        if (depth > maxDepth)\n            return;\n\n        const selector = precomputedSelector ?? await filteredSelectorForElement(element, includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers);\n        if (!selector)\n            return;\n\n        lines.push('\\t'.repeat(depth) + selector);\n\n        if (depth === maxDepth) {\n            if (element.children.length > 0)\n                lines.push('\\t'.repeat(depth + 1) + '…');\n            return;\n        }\n\n        const allChildren = Array.from(element.children);\n        const children = allChildren.slice(0, maxChildren);\n\n        let index = 0;\n        while (index < children.length) {\n            const signature = await filteredSelectorForElement(children[index], includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers);\n            if (!signature) {\n                index++;\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            let runLength = 1;\n            while (runLength < 10 && index + runLength < children.length && await filteredSelectorForElement(children[index + runLength], includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers) === signature)\n                runLength++;\n\n            if (runLength > 1) {\n                lines.push('\\t'.repeat(depth + 1) + signature + ' ×' + runLength);\n                index += runLength;\n            } else {\n                await walk(children[index], depth + 1, signature);\n                index++;\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (allChildren.length > maxChildren)\n            lines.push('\\t'.repeat(depth + 1) + '…');\n    }\n\n    const root = rootSelector ? document.querySelector(rootSelector) : document.body;\n    if (!root)\n        return { header: rootSelector ? 'Error: rootSelector did not match any element.' : 'Error: No document body.', content: '' };\n\n    if (rootSelector && document.querySelectorAll(rootSelector).length > 1)\n        return { header: 'Error: rootSelector matched multiple elements — use a more specific selector.', content: '' };\n\n    let startElement = root;\n    if (includeAncestors && rootSelector) {\n        let ancestor = root.parentElement;\n        let steps = 0;\n        while (ancestor && ancestor !== document.documentElement && steps < 3) {\n            startElement = ancestor;\n            ancestor = ancestor.parentElement;\n            steps++;\n        }\n    }\n\n    if (includeAncestors && rootSelector && startElement !== root) {\n        const path = [];\n        let node = root;\n        while (node) {\n            path.unshift(node);\n            if (node === startElement) break;\n            node = node.parentElement;\n        }\n\n        for (let i = 0; i < path.length - 1; i++) {\n            const element = path[i];\n            const depth = i;\n\n            if (i > 0) {\n                const parent = path[i - 1];\n                const idx = Array.from(parent.children).indexOf(element);\n                if (idx > 0)\n                    lines.push('\\t'.repeat(depth) + '…');\n            }\n\n            const selector = await filteredSelectorForElement(element, includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers);\n            if (selector) lines.push('\\t'.repeat(depth) + selector);\n        }\n\n        const rootDepth = path.length - 1;\n        const parentOfRoot = path[path.length - 2];\n        const rootSiblings = parentOfRoot ? Array.from(parentOfRoot.children) : [];\n        const rootIdx = rootSiblings.indexOf(root);\n\n        if (rootIdx > 0)\n            lines.push('\\t'.repeat(rootDepth) + '…');\n\n        await walk(root, rootDepth);\n\n        if (rootIdx >= 0 && rootIdx < rootSiblings.length - 1)\n            lines.push('\\t'.repeat(rootDepth) + '…');\n    } else {\n        await walk(startElement, 0);\n    }\n\n    let output = lines.join('\\n');\n    if (output.length > maxOutputLength) {\n        const cutPoint = output.lastIndexOf('\\n', maxOutputLength);\n        output = (cutPoint > -1 ? output.slice(0, cutPoint) : output.slice(0, maxOutputLength)) + '\\n… (truncated)';\n    }\n\n    return output;\n})();"
+ "\n\n    const skipTags = new Set(['script', 'style', 'noscript', 'head', 'meta', 'link', 'title']);\n    const landmarkRoles = new Set(['banner', 'complementary', 'contentinfo', 'form', 'main', 'navigation', 'region', 'search']);\n\n    async function buildSpecificSelector(element) {\n        if (includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers && element.getAttribute('id'))\n            return filteredSelectorForElement(element, includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers);\n\n        const elementSelector = await filteredSelectorForElement(element, includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers);\n        if (!elementSelector)\n            return null;\n\n        const parts = [elementSelector];\n\n        let ancestor = element.parentElement;\n        let steps = 0;\n\n        while (ancestor && ancestor !== document.documentElement && steps < 3) {\n            const ancestorSelector = await filteredSelectorForElement(ancestor, includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers);\n            if (!ancestorSelector)\n                return null;\n\n            parts.unshift(ancestorSelector);\n            steps++;\n\n            if (includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers && ancestor.getAttribute('id'))\n                break;\n\n            if (!includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers && landmarkRoles.has(ancestor.computedRole))\n                break;\n\n            ancestor = ancestor.parentElement;\n        }\n\n        return parts.join(' ');\n    }\n\n    if (!query.trim())\n        return { header: 'Error: Query must not be empty.', content: '' };\n\n    let regex;\n    let normalizedRegex = null;\n    try {\n        if (isRegex) {\n            const safeFlags = (flags || 'i').replace(/[gy]/g, '');\n            regex = new RegExp(query, safeFlags);\n\n            const normalizedQuery = query.replace(/\\\\\\\\/g, '\\\\');\n            if (normalizedQuery !== query)\n                normalizedRegex = new RegExp(normalizedQuery, safeFlags);\n        } else {\n            const specialChars = new Set('^$.*+?()[]{}\\\\|');\n            const escaped = Array.from(query).map((char) => specialChars.has(char) ? '\\\\' + char : char).join('');\n            regex = new RegExp(escaped, 'i');\n        }\n    } catch (error) {\n        return { header: 'Error: Invalid pattern — ' + error.message, content: '' };\n    }\n\n    if (!document.body)\n        return { header: 'Error: No document body.', content: '' };\n\n    function findCandidates(regexToTest) {\n        const results = [];\n        const walker = document.createTreeWalker(document.body, NodeFilter.SHOW_ELEMENT);\n\n        let node = walker.nextNode();\n        while (node) {\n            if (!skipTags.has(node.tagName.toLowerCase()) && regexToTest.test(node.textContent.replace(/\\s+/g, ' ').trim()))\n                results.push(node);\n            node = walker.nextNode();\n        }\n\n        return results;\n    }\n\n    let candidates = findCandidates(regex);\n    let usedFallback = false;\n\n    if (candidates.length === 0 && normalizedRegex) {\n        candidates = findCandidates(normalizedRegex);\n        if (candidates.length > 0)\n            usedFallback = true;\n    }\n\n    const effectiveRegex = usedFallback ? normalizedRegex : regex;\n\n    if (candidates.length > 500)\n        return { header: 'Error: Query is too broad — ' + candidates.length + ' elements matched. Narrow the search terms.', content: '' };\n\n    const mostSpecific = candidates.filter((element) =>\n        !candidates.some((other) => element !== other && element.contains(other))\n    );\n\n    if (mostSpecific.length === 0)\n        return { header: 'No elements found.', content: '' };\n\n    const seenSelectors = new Map();\n    const uniqueEntries = [];\n    for (const element of mostSpecific) {\n        const selector = await buildSpecificSelector(element);\n        if (!selector || seenSelectors.has(selector))\n            continue;\n\n        seenSelectors.set(selector, element);\n\n        const matchCount = document.querySelectorAll(selector).length;\n        let entry = selector + ' (' + matchCount + ' match' + (matchCount === 1 ? '' : 'es') + ')';\n\n        if (matchCount === 1) {\n            const text = element.textContent.replace(/\\s+/g, ' ').trim();\n            const filteredText = await filterText(text);\n            if (filteredText) {\n                const matchResult = effectiveRegex.exec(filteredText);\n                if (matchResult) {\n                    const half = Math.floor(maxContextLength / 2);\n                    const start = Math.max(0, matchResult.index - half);\n                    const rawEnd = Math.min(filteredText.length, matchResult.index + matchResult[0].length + half);\n                    const end = Math.min(filteredText.length, Math.max(matchResult.index + matchResult[0].length, Math.min(rawEnd, start + maxContextLength)));\n                    const snippet = (start > 0 ? '…' : '') + filteredText.slice(start, end) + (end < filteredText.length ? '…' : '');\n                    entry += ' \"' + snippet + '\"';\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        uniqueEntries.push(entry);\n    }\n\n    const total = uniqueEntries.length;\n    const lines = uniqueEntries.slice(0, maxResults);\n    if (total > maxResults)\n        lines.push('… (' + (total - maxResults) + ' more result' + (total - maxResults === 1 ? '' : 's') + ')');\n\n    const prefix = usedFallback ? 'Note: regex pattern was incorrectly double-escaped. Normalized for these results.\\n' : '';\n    const header = prefix + (total === 1 ? '1 result' : total + ' results') + ':';\n    return { header: header, content: lines.join('\\n') };\n})();"
+ "\n\n    function collectNames(rules) {\n        for (const rule of rules) {\n            if (names.size >= maxNames)\n                return;\n\n            try {\n                if (rule.style) {\n                    for (const prop of rule.style) {\n                        const trimmed = prop.trim();\n                        if (trimmed.startsWith('--'))\n                            names.add(trimmed);\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if (rule.cssRules)\n                    collectNames(rule.cssRules);\n            } catch (error) {\n                // Skip cross-origin or invalid rules.\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    for (const sheet of document.styleSheets) {\n        try {\n            collectNames(sheet.cssRules);\n        } catch (error) {\n            // Skip cross-origin stylesheets.\n        }\n    }\n\n    const filterTerms = terms?.length > 0 ? terms.map((term) => term.toLowerCase()) : null;\n    const computed = getComputedStyle(document.documentElement);\n\n    const sortedNames = [...names].sort();\n\n    const allLines = [];\n    for (const name of sortedNames) {\n        if (filterTerms && !filterTerms.some((term) => name.toLowerCase().includes(term)))\n            continue;\n\n        const rawValue = computed.getPropertyValue(name).trim();\n        if (!rawValue)\n            continue;\n\n        const filteredValue = await filterText(rawValue);\n        if (!filteredValue)\n            continue;\n\n        const truncated = truncateCSSValue(filteredValue);\n        if (!truncated)\n            continue;\n\n        allLines.push(name + ': ' + truncated);\n    }\n\n    if (!allLines.length)\n        return { header: 'No CSS custom properties found on :root.', content: '' };\n\n    const total = allLines.length;\n    const lines = allLines.slice(0, maxResults);\n    for (let i = lines.length - 1; i > 0; --i) {\n        const j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));\n        [lines[i], lines[j]] = [lines[j], lines[i]];\n    }\n\n    const header = total === 1 ? '1 CSS custom property:'\n        : total + ' CSS custom properties' + (total > maxResults ? ' (showing first ' + maxResults + '):' : ':');\n    return { header: header, content: lines.join('\\n') };\n})();"
+ "\n\n    function toKebabCase(string) {\n        return string.replace(/([A-Z])/g, '-$1').toLowerCase();\n    }\n\n    const element = document.querySelector(selector);\n    if (!element)\n        return { header: 'Error: No element matched selector.', content: '' };\n\n    const computed = window.getComputedStyle(element);\n    const allProperties = Array.from(computed);\n    const terms = searchTerms.map((term) => toKebabCase(term).toLowerCase());\n    const matching = allProperties.filter((prop) => {\n        if (searchMode === 'exactName')\n            return terms.some((term) => prop === term);\n\n        if (searchMode === 'exactValue') {\n            const value = computed.getPropertyValue(prop).trim();\n            return value && terms.some((term) => value === term);\n        }\n\n        if (searchMode !== 'values' && terms.some((term) => prop.includes(term)))\n            return true;\n\n        if (searchMode !== 'names') {\n            const value = computed.getPropertyValue(prop).trim();\n            return value && terms.some((term) => value.toLowerCase().includes(term));\n        }\n\n        return false;\n    });\n\n    function matchPriority(prop) {\n        for (const term of terms) {\n            if (prop === term)\n                return 0;\n\n            if (prop.startsWith(term + '-'))\n                return 1;\n\n            if (prop.endsWith('-' + term)) {\n                const prefix = prop.slice(0, prop.length - term.length - 1);\n                return 2 + (prefix.match(/-/g) || []).length;\n            }\n\n            if (prop.includes(term))\n                return 10;\n        }\n\n        return 20;\n    }\n\n    matching.sort((a, b) => matchPriority(a) - matchPriority(b));\n\n    if (!matching.length)\n        return { header: 'No properties matched search terms.', content: '' };\n\n    const lines = [];\n    for (const prop of matching) {\n        if (lines.length >= maxResults)\n            break;\n\n        const rawValue = computed.getPropertyValue(prop).trim();\n        if (!rawValue)\n            continue;\n\n        const filtered = await filterText(rawValue);\n        if (!filtered)\n            continue;\n\n        const truncated = truncateCSSValue(filtered);\n        if (!truncated)\n            continue;\n\n        lines.push(prop + ': ' + truncated);\n    }\n\n    if (!lines.length)\n        return { header: 'No property values returned.', content: '' };\n\n    for (let i = lines.length - + "Evaluate a JavaScript function against the current page and get back a boolean, number,\nor a short homogeneous array of booleans or numbers (max 4 elements).\nStrings and objects are never returned. Non-boolean, non-numeric return values are\ncoerced: strings parse as numbers if possible, else non-empty is true; arrays return their count.\n\nWrite a self-contained function body that inspects the page and returns a boolean or number.\nUse this for hypotheses that require imperative logic: conditional checks, arithmetic over\nelement attributes, multi-step DOM traversal, reading JavaScript state or framework globals,\nor anything the declarative probe tools cannot express.\n\nFunctions must be read-only — they may read any page state but must not modify the DOM, attributes,\nstyles, or storage, trigger user interactions, make network requests, or navigate. Any attempt to\ndo so will be rejected with an error.\n\nThe result is a single value: a boolean or number. Always use `return` to produce a\nvalue — `console.log` output is discarded and never returned.\n\nWORLD:\n- \"isolated\" (default): runs in an isolated JavaScript environment. The full DOM is accessible,\nbut the page's own scripts and globals are not — `window.*` variables and framework internals\ndefined by the page are not visible. Errors return \"Error: Probe failed.\".\n- \"main\": runs in the page's main JavaScript world. All page-defined globals are accessible\n(`window.*`, framework state, etc.). Errors return \"Error: Probe failed.\" — use this when\nyou need page JS scope and can write defensively.\n\nUse \"isolated\" for DOM inspection and \"main\" only when you specifically need to read JavaScript\nstate the page has defined.\n\nEXAMPLES:\n- Count items above a score threshold (isolated):\n  \"const rows = document.querySelectorAll('tr.athing'); let count = 0;\n  rows.forEach(r => { const s = r.nextSibling?.querySelector('.score');\n  if (s && parseInt(s.textContent) > 100) count++; }); return count;\"\n- Check whether a sticky header overlaps the viewport top (isolated):\n  \"const h = document.querySelector('header'); if (!h) return false;\n  return h.getBoundingClientRect().top === 0;\"\n- Check whether a React app has mounted (main):\n  \"return typeof window.React !== 'undefined';\"\n- Get the position of an element (isolated):\n  \"const el = document.querySelector('#banner'); if (!el) return [];\n  const r = el.getBoundingClientRect(); return [r.x, r.y];\"\n- Count grid columns in a container (isolated):\n  \"const el = document.querySelector('#grid'); if (!el) return 0;\n  const cols = getComputedStyle(el).gridTemplateColumns;\n  return cols === 'none' ? 0 : cols.trim().split(/\\\\s+/).length;\"\n- Check whether a container is scrollable (isolated):\n  \"const el = document.querySelector('.feed'); if (!el) return false;\n  return el.scrollHeight > el.clientHeight;\"\n- Count items in a list or grid (isolated):\n  \"return document.querySelectorAll('.card-item').length;\""

+ "Finds elements on the page whose full text content matches a plain-text string or\nregular expression. Returns a CSS selector and match count for each result. All\nresults are wrapped in sentinel tags marking them as untrusted page data.\n\nText matching aggregates all descendant text, so an element whose label is split\nacross child spans is still found correctly. Results are the innermost matching\nelements — the labeled control is returned rather than its containing section.\n\nEach returned selector is anchored to the nearest ID-bearing ancestor for specificity\nrather than returning a bare tag-and-class selector. The match count reflects how many\nelements on the page match that CSS selector. When a selector matches exactly one\nelement, a text snippet is included showing the match with up to 40 characters of\nsurrounding context (50 characters total).\n\nSet `isRegex: true` to search by regular expression — useful for matching numbers or\nmultiple string variants. Flags default to `i` (case-insensitive); `g` is ignored.\n\n**Regex escaping**: write patterns exactly as they appear between `/` slashes — single\nbackslashes for escape sequences. Do not double-escape: `\\\\(` matches a literal\nbackslash, not a parenthesis.\n\nBy default returns selectors using only tag names and browser-computed ARIA roles.\nPass `includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers: true` to include site-specific class names, IDs,\nand data attributes — useful when you need a precise selector for specific site markup.\nAncestor anchoring walks up to the nearest landmark role by default, or the nearest\nID-bearing element when site-specific identifiers are included.\n\nEXAMPLES:\n- Action button: query=\"Subscribe\", isRegex=false\n- Consent notice: query=\"cookie\", isRegex=false\n- Price elements: query=\"[$€£¥][\\d,]+\\.?\\d*\", isRegex=true\n- Sign-in variants: query=\"sign[ -]in|log[ -]in\", isRegex=true\n- Parenthesized count: query=\"\\(\\d+\\)\", isRegex=true"

+ "Returns computed CSS property values for an element on the current page. All results\nare wrapped in sentinel tags marking them as untrusted page data.\n\nThe first element matching `selector` is inspected via `getComputedStyle`, which\nreturns resolved values — not authored declarations. `color` returns `rgb(26, 26, 26)`,\nnot `var(--brand-color)`. Up to 20 matching properties are returned.\n\n`searchTerms` filters by property name or value (case-insensitive substring): \"color\"\nmatches `color`, `background-color`, `border-color`, etc.; \"gradient\" matches any\nproperty whose name or computed value contains \"gradient\". Exact and close matches are\nprioritized so they always appear in results even when many properties match. More\nspecific terms give less noisy results: \"border-radius\" over \"border\",\n\"mask-image\" over \"image\".\n\n`searchMode` controls what the terms match against (default `exactName`):\n- `exactName`: exact property name match — use when you know the specific property\n  (e.g. searching \"color\" for text color returns only `color: rgb(...)`, not every\n  color-related property). Prefer this when you know exactly what you want.\n- `names`: substring match on property names — use for a focused survey of related\n  properties (e.g. \"color\" for all color-related properties, \"flex\" for all flex\n  properties).\n- `both`: match against property names or values — use when the term may appear\n  in either (e.g. \"flex\" also finds `display: flex` via value match).\n- `values`: substring match on computed values only.\n- `exactValue`: exact value match — use when searching for properties set to a\n  specific known value (e.g. \"grid\" to find only `display: grid`).\n\nUse this to understand an element's current layout or appearance (e.g. inspect\n`display`, `flex-direction`, and `gap` on a container to understand why its children\nstack, or read color values to capture them as variables).\n\nEXAMPLES:\n- Text color of an element: selector=\".badge\", searchTerms=[\"color\"], searchMode=exactName\n- Layout of a grid container: selector=\".cards\", searchTerms=[\"display\", \"grid-template-columns\"], searchMode=exactName\n- All color-related properties: selector=\".card\", searchTerms=[\"color\"], searchMode=names\n- Is element using flexbox: selector=\"nav\", searchTerms=[\"flex\"], searchMode=both\n- Position and stacking: selector=\"#header\", searchTerms=[\"position\", \"z-index\"], searchMode=exactName"
+ "Returns structural information about the live page — tag names, class names, IDs, ARIA\nroles, and structural data attributes. All results are wrapped in sentinel tags marking\nthem as untrusted page data.\n\nUse `rootSelector` to scope the walk to a specific subtree. Must match exactly one\nelement — prefer an ID or a specific selector. Defaults to the document body when omitted.\n\nAdd `includeAncestors: true` to walk up to 3 levels above the matched element before\ndescending — use this to discover ancestor containers of a known element. Only applies\nwhen `searchTerms` is omitted; ignored when `searchTerms` is provided.\n\nWith `searchTerms` (preferred): returns only element chains where at least one element\nmatches a term in its tag name, class list, ID, role, or first data-attribute name or\nvalue. Each chain shows the match, its ancestors up to the nearest ID-bearing ancestor\n(max 3 steps), and its immediate children. Chains are separated by ---. Matched elements\ninclude a short text snippet (center-truncated to 50 chars). Use this mode whenever you\nknow what vocabulary to search for — it is more focused and token-efficient.\n\nWithout `searchTerms`: returns the full structural tree, truncated at 4000 characters.\nUse only when a broad survey is needed to discover the site's vocabulary before forming\ntargeted queries, or when prior targeted probes returned no results.\n\nConsecutive same-element runs are shown as ×N (e.g. \"li.nav-item ×5\"). Element order\nwithin a parent is preserved.\n\nBy default returns selectors using only tag names and browser-computed ARIA roles.\nPass `includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers: true` to include site-specific class names, IDs,\nand data attributes — useful when you need a precise selector for specific site markup."

+ "Runs a sub-agent that probes the page to discover and capture site-specific values —\nCSS selectors, XPath expressions, or CSS custom property names — and store them as named\nvariables. Returns variable names, types, match counts, and a scope (general or\nsite-specific) with the filename to reference. See the Scope section in Guidelines for\nhow to use the scope to structure the manifest.\n\n`query` — include both what and why: \"Find the cookie consent banner to hide it\" or\n\"Locate the article body and sidebar to apply layout changes.\" The purpose helps the\nsub-agent choose the right container level and avoid capturing redundant children.\nInclude questions about properties you anticipate needing — layout model, positioning,\nscroll behavior, color scheme, font properties — and the sub-agent will probe and\nattach them as observed facts. Only ask for what the request suggests you will need.\n\n`variableWords` — the English identifier words you plan to use in code. Variable names\nare assembled from these words combined with a built-in set of structural terms\n(container, wrapper, item, overlay, etc.). + "function selectorForElement(element, includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers) {\n    const maxClasses = 5;\n\n    let selector = element.tagName.toLowerCase();\n\n    if (includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers) {\n        const classes = Array.from(element.classList).slice(0, maxClasses);\n        if (classes.length)\n            selector += '.' + classes.map(CSS.escape).join('.');\n\n        const id = element.getAttribute('id');\n        if (id)\n            selector += '#' + CSS.escape(id);\n    }\n\n    if (element.tagName.toLowerCase() === 'input' && element.type !== 'text')\n        selector += '[type=' + element.type + ']';\n\n    if (element.tagName.toLowerCase() === 'button' && element.type !== 'submit')\n        selector += '[type=' + element.type + ']';\n\n    if (element.open)\n        selector += '[open]';\n\n    if (element.hidden)\n        selector += '[hidden]';\n\n    if (element.inert)\n        selector += '[inert]';\n\n    const popover = element.popover;\n    if (popover === 'auto' || popover === 'manual')\n        selector += '[popover=' + popover + ']';\n\n    if (element.checked)\n        selector += '[checked]';\n\n    if (element.selected)\n        selector += '[selected]';\n\n    if (element.multiple)\n        selector += '[multiple]';\n\n    if (element.disabled)\n        selector += '[disabled]';\n\n    if (element.required)\n        selector += '[required]';\n\n    const contentEditable = element.contentEditable;\n    if (contentEditable === 'true' || contentEditable === 'false')\n        selector += '[contenteditable=' + contentEditable + ']';\n\n    const computedRole = element.computedRole;\n    if (computedRole && computedRole !== 'generic' && computedRole !== 'none' && computedRole !== 'presentation')\n        selector += '[role=' + computedRole + ']';\n\n    if (element.getAttribute('aria-hidden')?.toLowerCase() === 'true')\n        selector += '[aria-hidden=true]';\n\n    if (element.getAttribute('aria-modal')?.toLowerCase() === 'true')\n        selector += '[aria-modal=true]';\n\n    const ariaExpanded = element.getAttribute('aria-expanded')?.toLowerCase();\n    if (ariaExpanded === 'true' || ariaExpanded === 'false')\n        selector += '[aria-expanded=' + ariaExpanded + ']';\n\n    const ariaSelected = element.getAttribute('aria-selected')?.toLowerCase();\n    if (ariaSelected === 'true' || ariaSelected === 'false')\n        selector += '[aria-selected=' + ariaSelected + ']';\n\n    const ariaCurrent = element.getAttribute('aria-current')?.toLowerCase();\n    if (ariaCurrent && ['page', 'step', 'location', 'date', 'time', 'true'].includes(ariaCurrent))\n        selector += '[aria-current=' + ariaCurrent + ']';\n\n    if (includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers) {\n        for (const attribute of element.attributes) {\n            if (attribute.name.startsWith('data-')) {\n                selector += attribute.value && attribute.value.length <= 40\n                    ? '[' + attribute.name + '=' + CSS.escape(attribute.value) + ']'\n                    : '[' + attribute.name + ']';\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    return selector;\n}\n\nconst safeTagNames = new Set([\n    'a', 'abbr', 'address', 'article', 'aside', 'audio', 'b', 'blockquote', 'body',\n    'br', 'button', 'canvas', 'caption', 'cite', 'code', 'col', 'colgroup', 'data',\n    'datalist', 'dd', 'del', 'details', 'dfn', 'dialog', 'div', 'dl', 'dt', 'em',\n    'fieldset', 'figcaption', 'figure', 'footer', 'form', 'h1', 'h2', 'h3', 'h4',\n    'h5', 'h6', 'head', 'header', 'hr', 'html', 'i', 'iframe', 'img', 'input', 'ins',\n    'kbd', 'label', 'legend', 'li', 'link', 'main', 'map', 'mark', 'menu', 'meta',\n    'meter', 'nav', 'noscript', 'object', 'ol', 'optgroup', 'option', 'output', 'p',\n    'picture', 'pre', 'progress', 'q', 's', 'samp', 'script', 'section', 'select',\n    'small', 'source', 'span', 'strong', 'style', 'sub', 'summary', 'sup', 'table',\n    'tbody', 'td', 'template', 'textarea', 'tfoot', 'th', 'thead', 'time', 'title',\n    'tr', 'track', 'u', 'ul', 'var', 'video', 'wbr',\n]);\n\nasync function filteredSelectorForElement(element, includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers) {\n    const semanticSelector = selectorForElement(element, false);\n    const specificSelector = includeSiteSpecificIdentifiers ? selectorForElement(element, true) : semanticSelector;\n\n    let selectorToFilter = null;\n    if (specificSelector !== semanticSelector)\n        selectorToFilter = specificSelector;\n    else if (!safeTagNames.has(element.tagName.toLowerCase()))\n        selectorToFilter = semanticSelector;\n\n    if (!selectorToFilter)\n        return semanticSelector;\n\n    const filteredSelector = await filterText(selectorToFilter);\n    if (filteredSelector)\n        return filteredSelector;\n    if (selectorToFilter === semanticSelector)\n        return null;\n    return semanticSelector;\n}"
+ "function truncateCSSValue(value) {\n    const trimmed = value.trim();\n    if (!trimmed)\n        return null;\n\n    const maxCSSValueLength = 250;\n    const maxStringLength = 50;\n    const cssValueProperties = ['color', 'width', 'opacity', 'transition-duration',\n        'grid-template-columns', 'flex', 'grid-template-rows', 'grid-template-areas'];\n\n    if (cssValueProperties.some((property) => CSS.supports(property, trimmed)))\n        return trimmed.length <= maxCSSValueLength ? trimmed : trimmed.slice(0, maxCSSValueLength) + '…';\n\n    if (trimmed.length <= maxStringLength)\n        return trimmed;\n\n    const half = Math.floor(maxStringLength / 2);\n    return trimmed.slice(0, half) + '…' + trimmed.slice(-half);\n}"

- "Evaluate a JavaScript function against the current page and get back a boolean or number.\nReturns only boolean or numeric primitives — strings, objects, and arrays are never returned,\neliminating prompt injection risk entirely. Non-boolean, non-numeric return values are\ncoerced: strings parse as numbers if possible, else non-empty is true; arrays return their count.\n\nWrite a self-contained function body that inspects the page and returns a boolean or number.\nUse this for hypotheses that require imperative logic: conditional checks, arithmetic over\nelement attributes, multi-step DOM traversal, reading JavaScript state or framework globals,\nor anything the declarative probe tools cannot express.\n\nFunctions must be read-only — they may read any page state but must not modify the DOM,\nattributes, styles, or storage. Common mutations (innerHTML assignment, appendChild,\nsetAttribute, classList.add, etc.) are detected and rejected with an error.\n\nThe result is a single value in {\"result\": <bool or number>}.\n\nWORLD:\n- \"isolated\" (default): runs in an isolated JavaScript environment. The full DOM is accessible,\nbut the page's own scripts and globals are not — `window.*` variables and framework internals\ndefined by the page are not visible. Errors return {\"error\": \"Probe failed.\"}.\n- \"main\": runs in the page's main JavaScript world. All page-defined globals are accessible\n(`window.*`, framework state, etc.). Errors return {\"error\": \"Probe failed.\"} — use this when\nyou need page JS scope and can write defensively.\n\nUse \"isolated\" for DOM inspection and \"main\" only when you specifically need to read JavaScript\nstate the page has defined.\n\nEXAMPLES:\n- Count items above a score threshold (isolated):\n  \"const rows = document.querySelectorAll('tr.athing'); let count = 0;\n  rows.forEach(r => { const s = r.nextSibling?.querySelector('.score');\n  if (s && parseInt(s.textContent) > 100) count++; }); return count;\"\n- Check whether a sticky header overlaps the viewport top (isolated):\n  \"const h = document.querySelector('header'); if (!h) return false;\n  return h.getBoundingClientRect().top === 0;\"\n- Check whether a React app has mounted (main):\n  \"return typeof window.React !== 'undefined';\""

- "function normalizeColor(value) {\n    var span = document.createElement('span');\n    span.style.color = value;\n    if (!span.style.length)\n        return null;\n\n    var host = document.createElement('div');\n    var shadow = host.attachShadow({ mode: 'open' });\n    shadow.appendChild(span);\n    document.documentElement.appendChild(host);\n\n    var normalized = window.getComputedStyle(span).color;\n    document.documentElement.removeChild(host);\n\n    return normalized;\n}\n\nfunction rgbLightness(rgb) {\n    var match = rgb.match(/\\d+/g);\n    if (!match || match.length < 3)\n        return null;\n\n    var r = parseInt(match[0]) / 255, g = parseInt(match[1]) / 255, b = parseInt(match[2]) / 255;\n    return (Math.max(r, g, b) + Math.min(r, g, b)) / 2 * 100;\n}\n\nfunction toKebabCase(string) {\n    return string.replace(/([A-Z])/g, function(char) { return '-' + char.toLowerCase(); });\n}\n\nvar element = document.querySelector(selector);\nif (!element)\n    return false;\n\nvar computed = window.getComputedStyle(element).getPropertyValue(toKebabCase(cssProperty));\nvar normalizedComputed = normalizeColor(computed) || computed;\nvar lightness = rgbLightness(normalizedComputed);\n\nreturn lightness !== null && lightness < lightnessThreshold;"
